9608   "\n\nThis event callback specifies one or more dynamically allocated input/output or output only parameters. For this reason, you should temporarily store all input/output and output only parameters that " "you allocate into local variables.  At the end of your callback function, after you have determined " "that you will not return an error from the callback, deallocate the current value of every input/output " "parameter and assign the new values from your temporary local variables to each input/output and output only " "parameter. 10568   "Instrument Prefix\n" "-----------------\n" "Enter a string that uniquely describes the instrument.  The prefix should consist " "of a two-character vendor code followed by non-white space characters that uniquely " "identify the driver.  A listing of these two-character vendor codes is found in the " "VXIplug&play specification VPP-9:Instrument Vendor Abbreviations.\n" "This string will prefix all external function names, attribute IDs, and value definitions.  " "It will also be the base name of the generated driver files.  Although the maximum " "length can be 31 characters, it is recommended that the prefix be relatively short.\n" "Example 1: For a National Instruments 123 DMM, the prefix may be \"ni123\"" "Example 2: For the 3000 series Tektronix oscilloscopes, the prefix may be \"tk30xx\"\n\n"

10583   "Expected ID Query Response\n" "--------------------------\n" "Enter the string that your instrument sends in response to an identification query.\n" "Note:  Be sure to enter the response string exactly (with spaces, commas, etc.) as the instrument will return it.  " "The driver uses this string to compare with the actual instrument response in order to determine that the correct " "instrument is being addressed.  The entire response string is not required. 10588   "Self-Test Response Contents\n" "---------------------------\n" "Select the expected data format in the instrument response buffer.  " "Instruments typically return data in one of three formats.  " "These formats are: code only, string only, and string and code. 10596   "Format Choices\n" "--------------\n" "Enter the format string for the firmware revision query response.  " "The format string should output only the firmware revision.  You may need to have other modifiers " "in the string but they must be discarded within the format string.  Example: %*[^,],%[^\\n] will " "discard the beginning string and output the second string as the firmware revision query response.  " "The wizard provides some of the common response formats.  If the instrument does not return data in " "one of these formats, select Custom and enter the custom format string in the Format String control.\n" "Example:  To format a SCPI response like \"National Instruments,123,000000,V1.1\" " "(where V1.1 is the firmware revision) use:\n" "             %*[^,],%*[^,],%*[^,],%[^\\n]\n" "(the first 3 strings will be discarded by the * modifier)\n\n"

After connecting,\n" "the client transmits the raw file data. Transfer is\n" "complete when the client disconnects. The file is\n" "created on the target machine at the specified path and\n" "with the specified timestamp.\n" "You can use the functions in support/yosemite.h to obtain\n" "timestamps for files and to transfer files from the client."

18450   "Show the recorded samples for the running program.\n" "    show samples               show recorded samples\n" "    show samples <function>    show recorded samples for <function>\n\n" "For the first form, the output consists of six columns:\n" "    Top T  Top %%  Cum %%  Tot T  Tot %%  Function\n" "where\n" "    Top T      the number of samples at the top of the stack\n" "    Top %%      Top T as a percentage of the total ticks\n" "    Cum %%      cumulative record of Top %%\n" "    Tot T      the number of samples anywhere on the stack\n" "    Tot %%      Tot T as a percentage of the total ticks\n" "    Function   the name of the function\n\n" "For the second form, the output consists of four columns:\n" "    Tot T  Tot %%  Line  Text\n" "where\n" "    Tot T      the number of samples anywhere on the stack\n" "    Tot %%      Tot T as a percentage of the total ticks\n" "    Line       the line number\n" "    Text       the source code"
